        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;

          margin: auto;

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }

        }

          flex-grow: 0;

          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);

          overflow-y: auto;

          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

<div class="select-container">

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





chromeos_shutdown calls bootstat_archive with a chronos-controlled target directory, which is used to copy a set of files from /tmp. Chronos can set up this target directory before bootstat_archive is executed to cause bootstat_archive to write arbitrary file contents through a symbolic link.



<span class="line"><!---->chromeos_shutdown calls bootstat_archive with a chronos-controlled target directory, which is used to copy a set of files from /tmp. Chronos can set up this target directory before bootstat_archive is executed to cause bootstat_archive to write arbitrary file contents through a symbolic link.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Google Chrome	107.0.5304.110 (Official Build) (64-bit) 



<span class="line"><!---->Google Chrome	107.0.5304.110 (Official Build) (64-bit) <!----></span>



<br>





Revision	2a558545ab7e6fb8177002bf44d4fc1717cb2998



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/2a558545ab7e6fb8177002bf44d4fc1717cb2998"><!---->Revision	2a558545ab7e6fb8177002bf44d4fc1717cb2998<!----></a>





-refs/branch-heads/5304@{#1202}



<span class="line"><!---->-refs/branch-heads/5304@{#1202}<!----></span>



<br>





Platform	15117.112.0 (Official Build) stable-channel eve



<span class="line"><!---->Platform	15117.112.0 (Official Build) stable-channel eve<!----></span>



<br>





Firmware Version	Google_Eve.9584.230.0



<span class="line"><!---->Firmware Version	Google_Eve.9584.230.0<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





Execute the following shell script, which will trigger a reboot.



<span class="line"><!---->Execute the following shell script, which will trigger a reboot.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





echo EXPLOIT > /tmp/disk-messages



<span class="line"><!---->echo EXPLOIT &gt; /tmp/disk-messages<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





for offset in `seq 0 60`; do



<span class="line"><!---->for offset in `seq 0 60`; do<!----></span>



<br>





        TGT=/var/log/metrics/shutdown.$(date --date="+$offset sec" '+%Y%m%d%H%M%S')



<span class="line"><!---->        TGT=/var/log/metrics/shutdown.$(date --date="+$offset sec" '+%Y%m%d%H%M%S')<!----></span>



<br>





        mkdir ${TGT}



<span class="line"><!---->        mkdir ${TGT}<!----></span>



<br>





        ln -s /var/log/messages ${TGT}/disk-messages



<span class="line"><!---->        ln -s /var/log/messages ${TGT}/disk-messages<!----></span>



<br>





done



<span class="line"><!---->done<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





dbus-send --print-reply --system --dest=org.chromium.PowerManager /org/chromium/PowerManager org.chromium.PowerManager.RequestRestart uint32:0 string:



<span class="line"><!---->dbus-send --print-reply --system --dest=org.chromium.PowerManager /org/chromium/PowerManager org.chromium.PowerManager.RequestRestart uint32:0 string:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Post-reboot, observe that the contents of /var/log/messages have been overwritten with the controlled ‘EXPLOIT’ value (later values are added as part of normal bootup, but the ‘EXPLOIT’ value should be the first line)



<span class="line"><!---->Post-reboot, observe that the contents of /var/log/messages have been overwritten with the controlled ‘EXPLOIT’ value (later values are added as part of normal bootup, but the ‘EXPLOIT’ value should be the first line)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





DETAILS



<span class="line"><!---->DETAILS<!----></span>



<br>





As part of shutdown, chromeos_shutdown will call bootstat_archive [1] with a parent directory of /var/log/metrics/. This directory is owned by chronos. The chronos user can set up directories matching the timestamp “/var/log/metrics/shutdown.$(date '+%Y%m%d%H%M%S')” which contain symbolic links. When bootstat_archive is then run as part of shutdown it will perform an unsafe copy from /tmp into this directory [2]. A controlled /tmp/disk-* file will be copied to /var/log/metrics/shutdown.[timestamp]/disk-* as root. This can result in arbitrary file writes as root during shutdown.



<span class="line"><!---->As part of shutdown, chromeos_shutdown will call bootstat_archive [1] with a parent directory of /var/log/metrics/. This directory is owned by chronos. The chronos user can set up directories matching the timestamp “/var/log/metrics/shutdown.$(date '+%Y%m%d%H%M%S')” which contain symbolic links. When bootstat_archive is then run as part of shutdown it will perform an unsafe copy from /tmp into this directory [2]. A controlled /tmp/disk-* file will be copied to /var/log/metrics/shutdown.[timestamp]/disk-* as root. This can result in arbitrary file writes as root during shutdown.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The above proof of concept will create 60 timestamped directories to allow for a slower shutdown (i.e the next minute of bootstat_archive runs). A file is created at  /tmp/disk-messages (an unused disk- filename) and a symlink at /var/log/metrics/shutdown.[timestamp]/disk-messages to control both the contents and the targeted file of the file write.



<span class="line"><!---->The above proof of concept will create 60 timestamped directories to allow for a slower shutdown (i.e the next minute of bootstat_archive runs). A file is created at  /tmp/disk-messages (an unused disk- filename) and a symlink at /var/log/metrics/shutdown.[timestamp]/disk-messages to control both the contents and the targeted file of the file write.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1] 



<span class="line"><!---->[1] <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromiumos/platform2/+/refs/heads/master/init/chromeos_shutdown#129



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromiumos/platform2/+/refs/heads/master/init/chromeos_shutdown#129"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromiumos/platform2/+/refs/heads/master/init/chromeos_shutdown#129<!----></a>



<br>





[2] 



<span class="line"><!---->[2] <!----></span>





https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromiumos/platform2/+/refs/heads/master/bootstat/bootstat_archive#26



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromiumos/platform2/+/refs/heads/master/bootstat/bootstat_archive#26"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/chromiumos/platform2/+/refs/heads/master/bootstat/bootstat_archive#26<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





Requirements



<span class="line"><!---->Requirements<!----></span>



<br>





- None



<span class="line"><!---->- None<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Impact



<span class="line"><!---->Impact<!----></span>



<br>





- Arbitrary file overwrite as root. Due to the late stage of this execution during system shutdown, this cannot be reasonably used as part of the current boot and therefore can only target files on disk (not, for example, files in /proc).



<span class="line"><!---->- Arbitrary file overwrite as root. Due to the late stage of this execution during system shutdown, this cannot be reasonably used as part of the current boot and therefore can only target files on disk (not, for example, files in /proc).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Recommendation



<span class="line"><!---->Recommendation<!----></span>



<br>





- Add --remove-destination to cp or change the target directory to one that cannot be controlled by chronos



<span class="line"><!---->- Add --remove-destination to cp or change the target directory to one that cannot be controlled by chronos<!----></span>

> I think the fix for this is to update bootstat to accept the destination path as a command line switch so there is no need to copy the results.



<span class="line"><!---->&gt; I think the fix for this is to update bootstat to accept the destination path as a command line switch so there is no need to copy the results.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





There are various non-root callers of `boostat` (or its equivalent library functions; and even a separate implementation in Chrome...). So you'd have to open up the permissions of the target directory too, which probably defeats the purpose.



<span class="line"><!---->There are various non-root callers of `boostat` (or its equivalent library functions; and even a separate implementation in Chrome...). So you'd have to open up the permissions of the target directory too, which probably defeats the purpose.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I think you either need to harden the copy (in `bootstat_archive`), like suggest in the OP, or else add some privilege delegation, so that we don't need such wide permissions for the file locations. The latter would be complex, since some of the bootstat entries need to be generated rather early, probably before we're running most D-Bus services.



<span class="line"><!---->I think you either need to harden the copy (in `bootstat_archive`), like suggest in the OP, or else add some privilege delegation, so that we don't need such wide permissions for the file locations. The latter would be complex, since some of the bootstat entries need to be generated rather early, probably before we're running most D-Bus services.<!----></span>

I wasn't aware of the non-root callers, so that makes sense.



<span class="line"><!---->I wasn't aware of the non-root callers, so that makes sense.<!----></span>

Adding "--remove-destination" is fine for solving symlink issues with the last path component of the copy operation, but we also need to take the mkdir into account. I think a tmpfiles.d rule for the parent path, plus some checks might do a reasonable job.



<span class="line"><!---->Adding "--remove-destination" is fine for solving symlink issues with the last path component of the copy operation, but we also need to take the mkdir into account. I think a tmpfiles.d rule for the parent path, plus some checks might do a reasonable job.<!----></span>

bootstat: Make bootstat_archive symlink resistant.



<span class="line"><!---->bootstat: Make bootstat_archive symlink resistant.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This makes it harder to use symlinks to confuse bootstat_archive.



<span class="line"><!---->This makes it harder to use symlinks to confuse bootstat_archive.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





BUG=chromium:1398989



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1398989" title="Security: ChromeOS On halt/reboot root file overwrite"><!---->BUG=chromium:1398989<!----></a>



<br>





TEST=bootstat_archive <path with symlink> &&



<span class="line"><!---->TEST=bootstat_archive &lt;path with symlink&gt; &amp;&amp;<!----></span>



<br>





  bootstat_archive <path without symlink>



<span class="line"><!---->  bootstat_archive &lt;path without symlink&gt;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

bootstat: Make bootstat_archive symlink resistant.



<span class="line"><!---->bootstat: Make bootstat_archive symlink resistant.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

  bootstat_archive <path without symlink>

        /*

        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;

          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
